75:["$","h3",null,{"id":"q-which-method-should-i-choose-for-my-perl-script","className":"x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl","children":["Q: Which method should I choose for my Perl script?",["$","$Ld",null,{"id":"q-which-method-should-i-choose-for-my-perl-script"}]]}]
76:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"A:"}]," For most cases, use Method 1 (Form Data) with the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"-F"}]," flag. 77:["$","h3",null,{"id":"q-how-do-i-handle-data-that-contains-both-spaces-and-quotes","className":"x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl","children":["Q: How do I handle data that contains both spaces and quotes?",["$","$Ld",null,{"id":"q-how-do-i-handle-data-that-contains-both-spaces-and-quotes"}]]}]

7a:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"A:"}]," All methods work with curl 7.0+ (released in 2000). The ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"--data @filename"}]," syntax is also very old and widely supported. 7b:["$","h3",null,{"id":"q-are-there-performance-differences-between-methods","className":"x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl","children":["Q: Are there performance differences between methods?",["$","$Ld",null,{"id":"q-are-there-performance-differences-between-methods"}]]}]
7c:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"A:"}]," Form data and quoted data have similar performance for small payloads. Form data has slightly more overhead due to multipart encoding but the difference is negligible (2-3ms). Temporary files add file I/O overhead (~10ms) but eliminate memory usage for large payloads. For high-frequency operations, quoted data with JSON is often fastest."]}]
7d:["$","h3",null,{"id":"q-can-i-combine-multiple-approaches-in-one-script","className":"x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl","children":["Q: Can I combine multiple approaches in one script?",["$","$Ld",null,{"id":"q-can-i-combine-multiple-approaches-in-one-script"}]]}]
7e:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"A:"}]," Absolutely.
